ar-writes-in-the-opening-paragraph-but-what-does-it-mean-is-there-something-unique-about-it-what-skills-do-em-data-scientists-em-need-to-be-productive-in-a-world-deluged-by-data-what-are-the-implications-for-scientific-inquiry-p-p-he-defines-data-science-as-being-essentially-the-systematic-study-of-the-extraction-of-knowledge-from-data-but-a-href-http-en-wikipedia-org-wiki-data-analysis-target-self-analyzing-data-a-is-something-people-have-been-doing-with-statistics-and-related-methods-for-a-while-why-then-do-we-need-a-new-term-like-data-science-when-we-have-had-statistics-for-centuries-the-fact-that-we-now-have-huge-amounts-of-data-should-not-in-and-of-itself-justify-the-need-for-a-new-term-p-p-in-short-its-all-about-the-difference-between-em-explaining-em-and-em-predicting-em-data-analysis-has-been-a-href-http-blog-irvingwb-com-blog-2013-05-data-science-and-complex-systems-html-generally-used-a-as-a-way-of-explaining-some-phenomenon-by-extracting-interesting-patterns-from-individual-data-sets-with-well-formulated-queries-data-science-on-the-other-hand-aims-to-discover-and-extract-em-actionable-em-knowledge-from-the-data-that-is-knowledge-that-can-be-used-to-make-decisions-and-predictions-not-just-to-em-explain-em-whats-going-on-p-p-the-raw-materials-of-data-science-are-not-independent-data-sets-no-matter-how-large-they-are-but-heterogeneous-unstructured-data-set-of-all-kinds-text-images-video-the-data-scientist-will-not-simply-analyze-the-data-but-will-look-at-it-from-many-angles-with-the-hope-of-discovering-new-insights-p-p-one-of-a-href-http-www-forbes-com-sites-danwoods-2012-02-16-ibms-anjul-bhambhri-on-what-is-a-data-scientist-the-problems-a-with-conducting-such-an-in-depth-exploratory-analysis-is-that-the-multiple-data-sets-that-are-typically-required-to-do-so-are-often-found-within-organizational-em-silos-em-be-they-different-lines-of-business-in-a-company-different-companies-in-an-industry-or-different-institutions-across-society-at-large-data-science-platf
